### [258] [Information Pathways in Online Science Communication: The Role of Platform Actors and News Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17249)
*Alexandros Efstratiou,Giuseppe Russo,Luca Luceri*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 研究发现，在COVID-19科学传播中，最具影响力的推特账号主要是医学或研究背景的个人，但存在一个协调网络不成比例地放大少数持反共识立场的专家观点。这些有影响力者推广的论文与新闻媒体报道的论文高度重叠，但存在关键差异：支持共识的专家主要与主流医学媒体报道的研究互动，而反共识专家更倾向于低质量、伪科学或阴谋论来源的论文。新闻媒体倾向于在社交媒体"超级传播者"突出科学论文后才进行报道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学在线讨论涉及专家、新闻媒体和社交媒体用户之间复杂的互动，但现有研究往往孤立地考察这些参与者，对他们如何共同塑造科学传播的理解仍然不足。本研究旨在通过COVID-19大流行案例，揭示这些不同参与者之间的相互作用和信息流动模式。

Method: 使用COVID-19大流行作为案例研究，分析了124万条推文和21.1万篇新闻文章，这些内容都引用了与大流行相关的科学论文。通过数据挖掘和网络分析方法，识别了不同参与者的互动模式、影响力结构和信息流动路径。

Result: 1. 最具影响力的推特账号主要是具有医学或研究背景的个人
2. 发现了一个协调网络，不成比例地放大少数持反共识立场（关于疫苗、封锁等话题）的知名专家
3. 这些有影响力者推广的论文与新闻媒体报道的论文高度重叠，但存在关键差异：支持共识的专家主要与主流医学媒体报道的研究互动，而反共识专家更倾向于低质量、伪科学或阴谋论来源的论文
4. 新闻媒体倾向于在社交媒体"超级传播者"突出科学论文后才进行报道

Conclusion: 研究揭示了科学传播中多层次的信息流动路径和协调放大结构，这些结构塑造了社交媒体和新闻媒体之间的科学传播。这些发现为了解更广泛的信息生态系统动态提供了新的见解，强调了不同参与者之间的复杂相互作用如何影响科学信息的传播和接受。

Abstract: Online discussions of science involve complex interactions among experts, news media, and social media users as they interpret and disseminate scientific findings. While prior work has examined these actors in isolation, their interplay in shaping science communication remains poorly understood. Using the COVID-19 pandemic as a case study, we analyze 1.24M tweets and 211k news articles that reference pandemic-related scientific papers. We find that the most influential Twitter accounts in this discourse are predominantly individuals with medical or research credentials. However, we also identify a coordinated network that disproportionately amplifies a small set of prominent credentialed experts who advance contrarian, anti-consensus positions on vaccines, lockdowns, and related topics. The papers promoted by these influential actors substantially overlap with those covered by news media, but with key differences: pro-consensus experts primarily engage with studies featured by mainstream and medical outlets, whereas contrarian experts align more closely with papers promoted by low-quality, pseudoscientific, or conspiratorial sources. Notably, news outlets tend to report on scientific studies after they have been highlighted by social media superspreaders. Together, these findings reveal multi-level pathways of information flow and coordinated amplification structures that shape science communication across social media and news, offering new insights into the dynamics of the broader information ecosystem.

### [259] [A spatio-temporal graph-based model for team sports analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17471)
*Camille Grange,Quentin Bourgeais,Rodolphe Charrier,Géraldine Del Mondo,Antoine Dutot,Eric Sanlaville,Ludovic Seifert*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 团队运动具有复杂的时空特性，分析难度大。研究旨在分析外部约束对战术的影响，特别是教练教学和防守初始位置的作用。

Result: 初步结果显示教练教学和防守初始位置对战术有显著影响。模型验证了这两个假设的有效性。

Conclusion: 该图模型能有效分析团队运动战术，未来可应用于篮球等其他运动，验证更多关于团队协调模式的假设。

Abstract: Team sports represent complex phenomena characterized by both spatial and temporal dimensions, making their analysis inherently challenging. In this study, we examine team sports as complex systems, specifically focusing on the tactical aspects influenced by external constraints. To this end, we introduce a new generic graph-based model to analyze these phenomena. Specifically, we model a team sport's attacking play as a directed path containing absolute and relative ball carrier-centered spatial information, temporal information, and semantic information. We apply our model to union rugby, aiming to validate two hypotheses regarding the impact of the pedagogy provided by the coach on the one hand, and the effect of the initial positioning of the defensive team on the other hand. Preliminary results from data collected on six-player rugby from several French clubs indicate notable effects of these constraints. The model is intended to be applied to other team sports and to validate additional hypotheses related to team coordination patterns, including upcoming applications in basketball.

</details>


### [260] [Temporal Narrative Monitoring in Dynamic Information Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17617)
*David Farr,Stephen Prochaska,Jack Moody,Lynnette Hui Xian Ng,Iain Cruickshank,Kate Starbird,Jevin West*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 提出一个系统导向框架，用于将新兴叙事建模为时间演化的语义结构，无需预先标签，通过整合语义嵌入、基于密度的聚类和滚动时间链接，在危机事件中实现信息环境的感知和理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 危机事件中的信息环境理解具有挑战性，因为领域变化快速且抽象。现有方法多关注通过分类方法或网络方法描述信息环境的快照，忽略了信息随时间变化的时序特性。

Method: 提出系统导向框架，整合语义嵌入、基于密度的聚类和滚动时间链接，将叙事表示为共享语义空间中持久但自适应的实体，无需预先标签规范。

Result: 在真实危机事件中应用该方法，通过分层聚类验证和时间生命周期分析评估系统行为，结果显示高聚类一致性，并揭示了异质叙事生命周期，包括短暂片段和稳定叙事锚点。

Conclusion: 该方法基于情境感知理论，通过将非结构化社交媒体流转化为可解释的时序结构化表示，支持信息环境的感知和理解，为动态信息环境中的监测和决策支持提供方法论。

Abstract: Comprehending the information environment (IE) during crisis events is challenging due to the rapid change and abstract nature of the domain. Many approaches focus on snapshots via classification methods or network approaches to describe the IE in crisis, ignoring the temporal nature of how information changed over time.
  This work presents a system-oriented framework for modeling emerging narratives as temporally evolving semantic structures without requiring prior label specification. By integrating semantic embeddings, density-based clustering, and rolling temporal linkage, the framework represents narratives as persistent yet adaptive entities within a shared semantic space. We apply the methodology to a real-world crisis event and evaluate system behavior through stratified cluster validation and temporal lifecycle analysis. Results demonstrate high cluster coherence and reveal heterogeneous narrative lifecycles characterized by both transient fragments and stable narrative anchors.
  We ground our approach in situational awareness theory, supporting perception and comprehension of the IE by transforming unstructured social media streams into interpretable, temporally structured representations. The resulting system provides a methodology for monitoring and decision support in dynamic information environments.

</details>


### [261] [Crisis-induced differences in attention towards Ukraine in Twitter 2008-2023](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17899)
*Mark Mets,Maximilian Schich,Peter Sheridan Dodds*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析2008-2023年28种语言中"乌克兰"在Twitter上的关注度变化，揭示了2014年和2022年两次俄罗斯入侵事件引发的不同语言群体关注模式，发现两个几乎不重叠的语言集群，反映了各国对乌克兰支持态度的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已有研究探讨了2014年和2022年俄罗斯入侵乌克兰期间社交媒体动态，但缺乏跨语言的纵向比较分析。本研究旨在填补这一空白，通过多语言视角理解全球对乌克兰冲突的关注模式差异。

Method: 采用DNA微阵列启发的制图方法，分析2008-2023年28种语言Twitter数据中"乌克兰"一词的相对关注度变化（相对于各语言基线频率的对数过表达）。这种方法能够在宏观尺度上可视化关注模式，同时揭示单一语言视角难以察觉的细微差异。

Result: 研究发现两个几乎不重叠的语言集群：一个在2014年达到关注高峰，另一个在2022年达到高峰，具有不同的起始和衰减模式，反映了各国对乌克兰支持意愿（或犹豫）的差异。该方法能够捕捉本地、中观和全球尺度的关注模式。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了令人担忧的不对称性：虽然公开数据可以近似全球关注模式，但完整无过滤的视角仍主要隐藏在主要社交媒体平台的封闭专有算法背后。这种制图方法为比较跨语言、用户群体、平台甚至历史印刷语料库的相对偏见提供了多功能工具。

Abstract: Aggression against Ukraine has drawn widespread international attention, particularly in the wake of the two Russian invasions into Ukrainian territory in 2014 and 2022. Although previous studies have examined social-media dynamics around these events, a comparative longitudinal data-driven view across languages is still missing. This article fills this gap by mapping added attention to "Ukraine" on Twitter in 28 languages from 2008 to 2023, using a deceptively simple DNA microarray-inspired cartography of log over-expression relative to each language's baseline frequency. This macro-scale visualization makes familiar events stand out while uncovering subtler patterns beyond the cognitive reach of any single-language saudience. Most strikingly, two nearly non-overlapping language clusters emerge, one peaking around 2014 and the other around 2022 with distinct onset and decay profiles that mirror national readiness (or reluctance) to support Ukraine. By capturing attention at local, meso, and global scales, our approach offers a versatile tool for comparing relative bias across languages, user subgroups, platforms, or even historical print corpora. Ultimately, our cartographic approach reveals a troubling asymmetry: while publicly accessible data allows for an approximation of global attention patterns, the complete and unfiltered view remains largely hidden behind the closed, proprietary algorithms of major social media platforms, granting a far more comprehensive access to understanding global information flows.

</details>


### [262] [Grievance Politics vs. Policy Debates: A Cross-Platform Analysis of Conservative Discourse on Truth Social and Reddit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17901)
*Yining Wang,Alhasan Abdellatif,Artemis Deligianni,Hannah Hok,Yusuf Mucahit Cetinkaya,Tugrulcan Elmas*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 首个大规模比较分析Truth Social与主流保守派Reddit社区的研究，发现Truth Social更关注不满叙事，Reddit更注重政策辩论，Reddit毒性更高但Truth Social政治话题参与度更高


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 了解替代性右倾平台如何重塑在线话语，比较Truth Social与主流保守派Reddit社区在话题、毒性和时间动态上的差异

Method: 使用FASTopic进行主题建模和LLM辅助细化，分析Truth Social前八个月与r/Conservative、r/conservatives、r/Republican等Reddit社区的主题流行度、毒性和时间动态

Result: Truth Social以不满和叙事驱动内容为中心，Reddit更关注政策辩论；Reddit毒性更高，在文化和领导人相关主题中达到峰值；尽管平台间有相似的事件驱动参与冲击，但Truth Social用户在政治话题上的基线参与比例更高

Conclusion: 研究揭示了替代性右倾平台如何重塑在线话语，Truth Social与Reddit保守社区在内容焦点、毒性和参与模式上存在明显差异，有助于理解不同平台如何影响政治讨论生态

Abstract: We present the first large-scale comparative analysis of Truth Social and the most popular conservative Reddit communities, r/Conservative, r/conservatives, and r/Republican. Using topic modeling with FASTopic and LLM-assisted refinement, we analyze topic prevalence, toxicity, and temporal dynamics across these communities during the first eight months of Truth Social. We find clear contrasts: Truth Social centers on grievance and narrative-driven content, while Reddit focuses more on policy debates. Toxicity is higher on Reddit and peaks in cultural and leader-focused topics. Despite similar event-driven participation shocks across platforms, Truth Social shows higher baseline proportions of users engaging with political topics. Our findings contribute to understanding how alternative right-leaning platforms reshape online discourse.

</details>
